SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[InstallationDate], [d].[IsActive], [d].[Name], [d].[RatedPowerKW], [d].[Type], [d].[ZoneId], [z].[Id], [z].[Area], [z].[BuildingId], [z].[Name], [z].[Type], [e0].[Id], [e0].[Current], [e0].[DeviceId], [e0].[PowerConsumptionKW], [e0].[Temperature], [e0].[Timestamp], [e0].[Voltage]
FROM [Devices] AS [d]
INNER JOIN [Zones] AS [z] ON [d].[ZoneId] = [z].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[Current], [e].[DeviceId], [e].[PowerConsumptionKW], [e].[Temperature], [e].[Timestamp], [e].[Voltage]
    FROM [EnergyReadings] AS [e]
    WHERE [e].[Timestamp] >= @__fiveMinutesAgo_0
) AS [e0] ON [d].[Id] = [e0].[DeviceId]
WHERE [d].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit)
ORDER BY [d].[Id], [z].[Id], [e0].[Timestamp] DESC

SELECT [e0].[Key] AS [Date], COALESCE(SUM([e0].[PowerConsumptionKW]), 0.0) AS [Consumption], AVG([e0].[Temperature]) AS [AvgTemp]
FROM (
    SELECT [e].[PowerConsumptionKW], [e].[Temperature], CONVERT(date, [e].[Timestamp]) AS [Key]
    FROM [EnergyReadings] AS [e]

SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[InstallationDate], [d].[IsActive], [d].[Name], [d].[RatedPowerKW], [d].[Type], [d].[ZoneId], [z].[Id], [z].[Area], [z].[BuildingId], [z].[Name], [z].[Type], [e0].[Id], [e0].[Current], [e0].[DeviceId], [e0].[PowerConsumptionKW], [e0].[Temperature], [e0].[Timestamp], [e0].[Voltage]
FROM [Devices] AS [d]
INNER JOIN [Zones] AS [z] ON [d].[ZoneId] = [z].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[Current], [e].[DeviceId], [e].[PowerConsumptionKW], [e].[Temperature], [e].[Timestamp], [e].[Voltage]
    FROM [EnergyReadings] AS [e]
    WHERE [e].[Timestamp] >= @__fiveMinutesAgo_0
) AS [e0] ON [d].[Id] = [e0].[DeviceId]
WHERE [d].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit)
ORDER BY [d].[Id], [z].[Id], [e0].[Timestamp] DESC
